  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_5629304d-d5f2-449e-b7d2-7009cedbdc61'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initAppleId();

      initializeSiwa();

<span id="freeTextContainer16848165418102151366">In this pulse-pounding Immortals After Dark tale, #1 New York Times bestselling author Kresley Cole delves into the darkest mysteries and deepest passions of Clan MacRieve. . .<br/><br/>A Beast In Torment<br/><br/>Uilleam MacRieve believed he’d laid to rest the ghosts of his boyhood.   <span id="freeText16848165418102151366" style="display:none">In this pulse-pounding Immortals After Dark tale, #1 New York Times bestselling author Kresley Cole delves into the darkest mysteries and deepest passions of Clan MacRieve. . .<br /><br />A Beast In Torment<br /><br />Uilleam MacRieve believed he’d laid to rest the ghosts of his boyhood. But when a brutal torture revives those ancient agonies and destroys his Lykae instinct, the proud Scot craves the oblivion of death. Until he finds her—a young human so full of spirit and courage that she pulls him back from the brink.<br /><br />A Beauty In Chains<br /><br />Seized for the auction block, Chloe Todd is forced to enter a terrifying new world of monsters and lore as a bound slave. When offered up to creatures of the dark, she fears she won’t last the night. Until she’s claimed by him—a tormented immortal with heartbreaking eyes, whose touch sets her blood on fire.<br /><br />A Full Moon On The Rise<br /><br />With enemies circling, MacRieve spirits Chloe away to the isolated Highland keep of his youth. But once he takes her to his bed, his sensual mate becomes something more than human, evoking his savage past and testing his sanity. On the cusp of the full moon, can he conquer his worst nightmare to save Chloe . . . from himself?</span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/268914261" />
    <a title="When Funmi Met Romance" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5615242-when-funmi-met-romance"><img alt="When Funmi Met Romance" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1572219419p2/5615242.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/268914261?book_show_action=true">Jan 28, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="When Funmi Met Romance" class="user" itemprop="url" name="When Funmi Met Romance" href="/user/show/5615242-when-funmi-met-romance">When Funmi Met Romance</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">EVERYONE. read it or die basically</span></div>

        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer268914261" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer496564955120985630"><b>MacRieve IAD #13: 5 STARS OF OH MY GOD</b><br/><br/>Lets start this review off with a celebratory twerk for this great novel. <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380368467ra/721061.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I would like to just say that this book is amazing. <s>freaking obviously</s> Read it, love it, review it...whatever. NOW, <b>STOP READING HERE</b> if you can't take a spoiler because I'm about to spoil your worllllllld. I know what you're thinking, just use the spoiler html formatting thingy...well no. I hate how that looks. KAY NOW FOR THE FUN PART.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/602912.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> OH. MY. LORD.<br/><br/>This book was everything the doctor</span>
  <span id="freeText496564955120985630" style="display:none"><b>MacRieve IAD #13: 5 STARS OF OH MY GOD</b><br><br>Lets start this review off with a celebratory twerk for this great novel. <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380368467ra/721061.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I would like to just say that this book is amazing. <s>freaking obviously</s> Read it, love it, review it...whatever. NOW, <b>STOP READING HERE</b> if you can't take a spoiler because I'm about to spoil your worllllllld. I know what you're thinking, just use the spoiler html formatting thingy...well no. I hate how that looks. KAY NOW FOR THE FUN PART.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/602912.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> OH. MY. LORD.<br><br>This book was everything the doctor ordered. Unfortunately for me, KC has been giving me a huge heaping of disappointment lately. I tried to get in to her Arcana Chronicles series with her debut YA novel , Poison Princess. However, I ended up DNFing it which was the biggest shocker ever. As everyone knows, I'm a complete KC fangirl freakazoid. That being said, DNFing a novel by KC was akin to being stabbed in the heart. Then, the second blow was her Shadow's Claim novel which i actually had lukewarm feelings toward. That being said, I approached this Macrieve book with a modicum of apprehension. However, it was a just a fabulous as her other 12 IAD novels and kept me on my toes. <br><br>I've always adored how she writes Lykae. They brood the best, sound the best, seemingly look the best, screw the best, and well...are just generally the best in my opinion. There is nothing like a KC valkyrie or Lykae. SHE WROTE THE HELL OUT OF THIS NOVEL. MacRieve, or Will, was a man after my own heart. <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380368467ra/721062.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> I hated him at times and loved him at times. Which , I think is the mark of good writing. Similarly, I really liked Chloe. I didn't think I would like her. She's butcher than most romance heroines. Also, naturally, like most people who read romance novels I tend to be overly critical of my heroines. A trait i really must overcome. However, I ended up adoring chloe. She had spunk and intellgience. Similarly, she knew when to forgive, when to rage, and when to love. Her timing was impeccable and her feelings were understood. The fact that she ended up being a succubus was crazzzzzzzy. I'll admit that I didn't see that coming. However, I totally should have. It was nice being introduced to a new species. The fact that chloe ended up being Webb's daughter was HELLA PRICELESS. all i have to say is KC <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380368467ra/721063.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> kc, is you okay because that was so crazy!<br><br>Anywho, MacRieve pulled it together and Chloe and his reunion was freaking lovely and lit up. As far as steam goes, I must sadly admit that it was no where near the steam that we experienced as readers during Lothaire. Love it or hate that book, the sex in lothaire was so freaking raunchy and creative it had a girl turning up the AC! . However, the sex was still pretty damn good. <br><br>Now, lets talk about that FREAKING CLIFF HANGER!<img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380368467ra/721064.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> I can't believe it ended off like that. HOLY MOLY. Firstly, I kinda slept on the fact that Munroe was even going to get a book. You see, similar to many of you all, I'm chopping at the bits to get to Nix's book. The two books I craved more than anything were Lothaire (CHECK) and now Nix. I excitedly await all books, and I must admit my curiosity for Lanthe and her man almost know no bounds, however, NIX's book keeps me at night. Ok, not really, but It might tonight! So, now I know that more than likely, we will have to wait for, Furie and Kristoff, Lanthe and her Vrekner, and Munroe and his rather illfated human/werewolf basketcase.... THATS THREE BOOKS. At her pace of one book a year that means that we could possibly not know about nix until the year 2016-2017. I might perish. <br><br><b>Now for the crazy spoiler predictions that if you don't want to kind of figure out my thoughts on Nix's mate then you should stop reading now. I beg you, don't let me be the ruiner of your series, even If there is a chance that I'm wrong!</b><br><br>Oh kay dooookie. I beleve, in my heart of hearts, that Nix and Webb are mates. I'm not usually wrong about televison and literature predictions. Also, I had been mulling over this for a while. It makes complete and total sense. Firstly, nix is the beloved character. Moret than likely, the series will end ( i know just saying that this series could end makes me want to chain KC to a microsoft word document as my paranormal romance writer slave....okay that might have been overboard) on Nix's book. That being said, it would make sense that her book needs to go out with a fudging bang. Secondly, Nix is the biggest power player in the game. It seems fitting that she mate with Webb another HUGE POWERPLAYER. It would be hella ironic that the woman who helps all would go for the man who hurts all. Then, this book unveiled the shocker of the year, which not to be cocky I kind of suspected, that webb is FUCKING IMMORTAL. He is by far the most unstable and strong lorean anomaly ever IMHO. I mean he has about 4-5 different species in him. He's got lothaire, a fey, malkolm, and Ullieam in him. I mean DAMN. He is fucking lorean mixed drink. Also, he is freaking crazzzzzy. He sounds like the hitler of the lore. Not to mention nix said that he couldn't be harmed. And he mentioned being crossed by an ally. The only major ally who crosses anyone is nix. WHEW, glad I got all that out.<br><br><br>I'm dying to know everything about this series. There are so many matings and theories bumping through my head as You can see by my jumbled review. I aplogize for the spoilers if you didn't heed my warning. I also apologize for the grammar. I'm too excited after just finishing this book and I'm also tired. Therefore, I wouldn't be surprised to wake up and find out that this review is just one big ol' run on sentence. In conclusion, I loved this book and totally recommend it! <br><br><br><br><br><br><b>update: 6-29-2013</b> ITS ALMOSTTTTTTT HEREEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEEE BE EXCITED FANS<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380368467ra/721065.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>UPDATE: 6-1-2013</b> THIS HAS SPOILERS REGARDING THE EXCERPT<br><br>Okay, so KC has released the excerpt from chapter three i believe. Also, she released a huge excerpt of a full chapter 7, HOWEVER, one must buy a copy (kindle version) of The warlord Wants (i cant remember the full name) which is .99 cents on Amazon. I opted out of that beceause I'm a cheapskate. Anywho, IT WAS A DAMN GOOD EXCERPT. I had noooo freaking idea that Ullieam's excistance was shrouded in such sadness. It Hurt my heart It did. We'll see if I like the heroine. I have no idea if I do or not because the excerpt focused little on her. All we know is that she plays soccer (futbol) and she's transforming into SOMETHING. KC said it was something we haven't encountered so that rules out demons, vamp, valkyrie, sorceress, and witch. However, i'm scared because I don't believe in this point of the book Ulieman has experienced his Vivisection and stint in the Center!!! :[[[[ I have a feeling that our hearts will be breaking during this book, but I have faith in KCs ability to give a good story and a HEA. Well, heres to hoping that this is better than her last book shadow's claim... :)<br><br><br><br><br><b>UPDATE: 2-19-2013</b><br>So I might be late but whatever. I just read the full description for the book which releases a lot of GASP-worthy details. I think I'm gonna love this book. I pretty much hated the last book, she wrote for the spin off series, However this one sounds like its back to the KC i've grown to love.<br><br>1. the hero is a tortured , brooding, scot lykae.<br>2. The heroine has gone through adversity and is human<br><br>YAY, it seems like it will be a combination of Lothaire and Conrads book as far as themes go , I think. I'm excited. THOUGHTS, CONCERNS ?????<br><br><br><br><br>UPDATE COVER!!!!!!!!!!!!!!! HATE IT lol<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1360517706l/8158992.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>OMG WHY DOES IT LOOK LIKE THE GUY FROM THE WEN HAIR CARE INFOMERCIALS. EWWWWWWW<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380368467i/721066.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>July 9 2012 from her FB and Twitter:<br><br><b>UPDATE: 11-29-12</b><br><br>On her twitter, KC said that Uilleam's mate is a species NEVER mentioned BEFORE!!!!!! OMG the possibilities are endless!!!!!!!<br><br><br><blockquote>S&amp;S website, my nemesis, you’ve scooped me again! :) Yes, my next IAD hardcover is titled MACRIEVE and yes, it’s coming out May 14th. <br><br>Don’t worry—Nix, Lanthe, and Furie will all get books! But Uilleam’s story fits better into the overall Accession timeline (plus my editor is jonesing for poor Uilleam, who we last saw escaping from the facility.) More news soon!</blockquote><br><br>OMGGGGGGGGGGG , im so damn excited you have no idea. I'm obsessed <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/465723.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer2667376350115822099">2.5 stars. I was all into this book in the beginning. Its dark undertones appealed right away and then when Will first meets his Chloe, it was a lot of badassery with a touch of love struck wolf. I was eating it all right up. Then... something happens that made Will do a 180. While I get the dude was hurt by his past, he takes it out so badly on that poor girl that I was legit wishing for a separation and dissolution. I'm talking about next level douchedom happening to a girl who has lost EVERYT</span>
  <span id="freeText2667376350115822099" style="display:none">2.5 stars. I was all into this book in the beginning. Its dark undertones appealed right away and then when Will first meets his Chloe, it was a lot of badassery with a touch of love struck wolf. I was eating it all right up. Then... something happens that made Will do a 180. While I get the dude was hurt by his past, he takes it out so badly on that poor girl that I was legit wishing for a separation and dissolution. I'm talking about next level douchedom happening to a girl who has lost EVERYTHING. It gets bad enough for her that her life is in danger. That was the biggest turnoff. Ugh. Do they reconcile? Yes, but by then the infinitesimal effort he puts into the reunion makes absolutely no difference to me. His turnaround was completely conditional on one thing and I call BS. All my stars are for Chloe for her spunk, smart mouth, drive, and for breaking the mold people wanted her to fit. Will can go into the flames with my blessing. Safety: I would consider what the H does to Chloe emotional abuse. There is rape. </span>

I vow it to the Lore. Thirteen books in and I'm still reading the series?!<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380383701ra/742017.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>When I'm reading a new IAD installment:<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380383702ra/742018.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380383702ra/742019.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></b><br/><br/>I devour the words because Kresley Cole is just crazy good.<br/><br/><u>How so?</u><br/><br/>I've been wanting Lanthe and Thronos' story for <i>ages</i>...I'm not even going to go to Nix because her story I expect to be epic and she's a special </span>
  <span id="freeText3461581205873762932" style="display:none"><b>
  <u>WARNING: FANGIRL REVIEW</u>
</b><br><br><b>My reaction anytime I hear a new IAD installment is coming out:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380383701ra/742016.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Me when I get my hands on any new Kresley Cole, she's a goddess among authors, I say. I vow it to the Lore. Thirteen books in and I'm still reading the series?!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380383701ra/742017.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When I'm reading a new IAD installment:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380383702ra/742018.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380383702ra/742019.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></b><br><br>I devour the words because Kresley Cole is just crazy good.<br><br><u>How so?</u><br><br>I've been wanting Lanthe and Thronos' story for <i>ages</i>...I'm not even going to go to Nix because her story I expect to be epic and she's a special case. She'll need time to fully cook her masterpiece swan song.<br><br>So let's just say I have a major case of blue balls for Lanthe/Thronos. My non existent ballocks...ache for their story.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380383702ra/742020.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So when I learned that the next story after Lathaire's was going to be a Lykae story and <i>another</i> MacRieve at that..let's just say I was not the happiest camper.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380383702ra/742021.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So I expected to enjoy the story but not fully because I want Lanthe/Thronos action.<br><br>Consider me surprised with how touching Ullieam is. How much I craved his story and I didn't even know it. I can honestly say this was a turn in the right direction. And this twin arc/thing started...I'm too intrigued to not want it finished. Please don't make me wait two years for the next one.<br><br>Ullieam he's so damaged and I did not expect the depth of his angst. I was so angry, saddened and upset with what happened. All those emotions in just a prologue?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380383702ra/742022.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Seriously my feels list is long with this book. It goes all over the place. <br><br>And Chloe was such a fitting mate for Macrieve. She was such a kind person, totally did not see her being the species she turned out to be. But her species was so interesting to learn about. <br><br>Chloe is a smart ass, Ullieam is a damaged, possessive ass. We get to meet a handful of new characters, we get Nix crumbs (I love that crazy bitch!), a trip back to Scotland and glimpses of the next book set up. There's hot sex, crazy plot twists and fitting HEA. My favorite thing about the couple? The ease they had when they actually communicated, they had each other's back 100% and it was just really nice. An athlete heroine with no sinister secrets, I thought it was a nice change of pace.<br><br>My favorite quote? The entire book. Down to every period, comma, quotation mark...everything. Still fresh hilarious, serious, crazy good writing...still deliciously Kresley Cole.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380383702ra/742023.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>And the way the story ended?</b><br><br>-Chloe and Ullieam - they deserved each other and once again I lurve another MacRieve Lykae. He's not my favorite Lykae. That spot seems to be reserved by <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Garreth &lt;3 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> But I have a feeling Munro might shake up my Lykae fave hierachy. My favorite hero will forever be Cadeon, my sexy demon. (with Malkolm on the side)<br><br>-The cliffhanger ending - <i>holy shite</i> is it going to be a doozy. <br><br>Kresley Cole?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380383702ra/742024.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Just please don't make the next one umpteen months later.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/637250.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>My rating: 4.5 stars</b><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_364746073" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/364746073" />
    <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie"><img alt="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514769932p2/3275325.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/364746073?book_show_action=true">Jul 09, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie">Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781476713359" href="/book/show/15801738-macrieve">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=read-in-2013">read-in-2013</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer364746073" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15762103629066284442">Uilleam MacRieve, aka Will, aka MacRieve, is a haunted, tortured Lykae who has not ever been able to get over his past. Oh yes, he's tried to run, block it out, sex it out and drink it out but nothing has worked. Then he gets a call from Nucking-Futs Nïx, aka Nïx the Ever-Knowing, and a whole new chain of events are set in motion. <br/><br/>The one thing that KC can do oh-so-well is "the chase". I don't think I've ever read another series where it's been handled so well and so thoroughly. I've read a few </span>
  <span id="freeText15762103629066284442" style="display:none">Uilleam MacRieve, aka Will, aka MacRieve, is a haunted, tortured Lykae who has not ever been able to get over his past. Oh yes, he's tried to run, block it out, sex it out and drink it out but nothing has worked. Then he gets a call from Nucking-Futs Nïx, aka Nïx the Ever-Knowing, and a whole new chain of events are set in motion. <br><br>The one thing that KC can do oh-so-well is "the chase". I don't think I've ever read another series where it's been handled so well and so thoroughly. I've read a few complaints of this being the same ol, same ol and I guess if I was reading the books back to back that might be a problem but after a year wait, I am <i>"ravening"</i> for it! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/604214.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I really enjoy reading about tortured heroes and MacRieve certainly fits the bill. But...but, he is a teensy bit of a meanie. You would think after reading <i>Lothaire</i>, I would be over it but apparently not. Once he finds out about Chloe...he is way too harsh. Some of that is understandable but I just felt it was a bit over the top. <br><br>Chloe was wonderful and just very go with the flow and as she likes to say "rub some dirt in it". I loved that! I think with everything she goes through, she would have to be one tough cookie. I hated how she was treated and left to figure out everything on her own. <br><br>And then there's Munro! I LOVE him!! Obviously, almost nothings better than some yummy Scottish Alpha weres but throw in a soft side and I'm a goner! We do get a tiny glimpse of his story in the Epilogue...it sounds very interesting. Oh yes...I love Munro's and MacRieve's nicknames...<br><br><b>Hot...<i>and</i> Hotter???</b> Count me in!!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/490079.gif" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There is a ton of sexual tension and some steamy scenes and once you find out about Chloe, you will know why. I do wish there was a more romance but oh well, guess you have to make do with the dirty talker, MacRieve. <br><br>We also get the ongoing back story which I thought was interesting but almost a little far-fetched. Not sure I'm buying it but I'm going to withhold judgment for now. I do LOVE Nïx's involvement but it's almost become the norm instead of being surprised by it. <br><br>We did get to meet some new Lykaes and "other" creatures that could possibly have stories in the future...you never know. I was disappointed not to get some of my yummy Lothaire. It would have been icing on the cake. <br><br>Hopefully, Munro's story is up next but we will probably have to wait a year! Either way, I'll be ready. And if you enjoyed <i>Poison Princess</i>, there is an excerpt for the next book in the series, <i>Endless Knight</i>, with the yummy Cajun...can't wait for the book!<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379795000i/599584.png" width="400" height="050" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Favorite quotes:<br><br>♦ "She wore a neon pink T-shirt with big bold letters: S L U T <br><br>In smaller text below that: SEXUALLY LIBERATED UNINHIBITED TART."<br><br>♥ "She's your lucky penny."<br><br>♥ "Lick it like a candy cane."<br><br>♥ "Is my fierce female directing me to lower the boom?"</span>
  <a data-text-id="15762103629066284442" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/108233591?book_show_action=true">Jul 10, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">paranormal romance fans, tortured hero lovers</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=favorite-or-autobuy-author">favorite-or-autobuy-author</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=fated-to-be-mated">fated-to-be-mated</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=tortured-hero">tortured-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1570669-danielle-the-book-huntress-back-to-the-books?shelf=children-in-danger-harmed">children-in-danger-harmed</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer108233591" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5920801118437620176">MacRieve follows up the story arc of the Order and in a huge way. I loved how Cole ties things together. Who would have thunk the Lore community would be so connected. <br/><br/>MacRieve might be one of the most tortured IAD heroes. His experiences as a preteen damaged him severely and as such, he has no hope of finding his mate or for his matehood to be normal. And it also gave him a violent hatred for succubi, which is going to be a problem. When he hears that there is a young woman that everyone wants </span>
  <span id="freeText5920801118437620176" style="display:none">MacRieve follows up the story arc of the Order and in a huge way. I loved how Cole ties things together. Who would have thunk the Lore community would be so connected. <br /><br />MacRieve might be one of the most tortured IAD heroes. His experiences as a preteen damaged him severely and as such, he has no hope of finding his mate or for his matehood to be normal. And it also gave him a violent hatred for succubi, which is going to be a problem. When he hears that there is a young woman that everyone wants because she's Webb's daughter (the leader of the Order-a group of humans who are out to exterminate all the Loreans), he shows up to get revenge on his enemy, and isn't above using his daughter, and recognizes his mate. That's not the beginning of a happy ever after. No there is a lot of pain ahead.<br /><br />At times, MacRieve was a real mean bastard. I had to remind myself how damaged his was from his youthful experiences with a succubus. It didn't condone the way he treats Chloe, but it does give me understanding into why he was behaving that way. I did like how beautifully he changes and convincingly loves Chloe. I just wish he had done so a little sooner.<br /><br />I loved Chloe. This is one of those instances where the heroine makes the book. She was awesome. I don't know much about Soccer, but she made me look up some women soccer players. I liked that she was very focused on her soccer and was fearless on the field despite her small size. That determination served her in good stead in her experiences with MacRieve.<br /><br />I did also love hanging out with the New Orleans compound Lykae, including MacRieve, his brother Munro and the two young Lykae they are fostering until they get control of their wolves. I gained a lot more insight into the world of the Lykae with this book, and it was enlightening and fun. The world has gotten bigger with each book, and I find it more fascinating the more I learn about the Lore.<br /><br />I wasn't really that interested in MacRieve before I read this book, but i could hardly put it down. MacRieve did win me over, but I think I loved Chloe even more than I loved him. I'm glad that he found his mate and that they realized how much they loved each other. I'm verra curious to see what will happen with Munro and his mate.</span>

<div id="review_365209111" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/365209111" />
    <a title="Ren Puspita" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3666031-ren-puspita"><img alt="Ren Puspita" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1531111155p2/3666031.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/365209111?book_show_action=true">Jul 10, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ren Puspita" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ren Puspita" href="/user/show/3666031-ren-puspita">Ren Puspita</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Mass Market Paperback 9781451649925" href="/book/show/18404870-macrieve">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3666031-ren-puspita?shelf=own-and-read">own-and-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3666031-ren-puspita?shelf=abused-character">abused-character</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3666031-ren-puspita?shelf=own-mass-market">own-mass-market</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3666031-ren-puspita?shelf=ass-kick-heroine">ass-kick-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3666031-ren-puspita?shelf=annoying-chara">annoying-chara</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3666031-ren-puspita?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3666031-ren-puspita?shelf=enemy-to-lover">enemy-to-lover</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3666031-ren-puspita?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3666031-ren-puspita?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3666031-ren-puspita?shelf=demon">demon</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer365209111" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1616964677784310294"><b>3.5 stars</b><br/><br/><b>EDIT: I reduce the stars, because... <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18775652.Dark_Skye__Immortals_After_Dark__14_' title='Dark Skye (Immortals After Dark #14) by Kresley Cole' rel='nofollow noopener'><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1389467343s/18775652.jpg' alt='Dark Skye (Immortals After Dark #14) by Kresley Cole' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></a> is FULL OF AWESOME and kinda antithesis with MacRieve. Sorry Chloe! (But no sorry for you Will! Heh :P)</b><br/><br/>With so many paranormal romance authors work out there (even I know that some people think that PNR and UF now become less popular compare to the latest trend), Kresley Cole is one of those authors that still shine in the pararomancelandia (my term) and her Immortals After Dark seroes will always be my guilty pleasure read!<br/><br/>For me, I never become a </span>
  <span id="freeText1616964677784310294" style="display:none"><b>3.5 stars</b><br><br><b>EDIT: I reduce the stars, because... <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18775652.Dark_Skye__Immortals_After_Dark__14_" title="Dark Skye (Immortals After Dark #14) by Kresley Cole" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1389467343s/18775652.jpg" alt="Dark Skye (Immortals After Dark #14) by Kresley Cole" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> is FULL OF AWESOME and kinda antithesis with MacRieve. Sorry Chloe! (But no sorry for you Will! Heh :P)</b><br><br>With so many paranormal romance authors work out there (even I know that some people think that PNR and UF now become less popular compare to the latest trend), Kresley Cole is one of those authors that still shine in the pararomancelandia (my term) and her Immortals After Dark seroes will always be my guilty pleasure read!<br><br>For me, I never become a fans of Lykae (don't throw something on me!) and prefer the vampires of IAD series (they're yummy. And lovable. And devoted. And less jerk). From Lachlan (who to much have macho vibe), Bowen (who said another woman name when he had sex with Mariketa. Ick!), to Garreth (who... I don't remember his story to be honest :P) and now into Uilleam MacRieve. Longtime fans of IAD already know him and his twin Munro from A Hunger Like No Other. Known as Hot and Hotter, these twins stole fans attention. Especially Ulliam after the event from Demon from the Dark, when he got tortured, vivisected, and meet his nightmare in the form of succubus. We don't know why, but readers will finally find the answer in MacRieve.<br><br>The story begin with a glimpse into Uilleam's horrible past, as he become victim of a succubae. Fast forward centuries later and the past still haunted him. With Uilleam still recovered from his torture and Munro become desperate to save his stubborn vampire, they got news that the witches captured Commander Webb's daughter. Bend on his revenge, Uilleam and Munro go to the auction, just to realize that his enemy's daughter is his mate.<br><br>Chloe Todd have a bright future as a soccer athlete, but her world turn upside down after she become auctioned for thing that she doesn't understand. Lucky for Chloe because Uilleam save her and claimed Chloe as her mate. But, fate is a bitch and she throw another challenge to this new couple with Chloe suddenly reach her maturity and become...succubus. A bad news for Uilleam indeed, for he can't fight his instinct, yet Chloe is everything that he despised. <br><br>I really dislike Uilleam and I don't get why he insist everyone to call him MacRieve. I think he never did that in previous books. He's a jerk, over and over. Not just to Chloe, but Munro as well! I know that his childhood past was so fucked up,and sometimes time can't heal a wound deep in the heart. But, really, 9 centuries and Uilleam still act as coward, still not brave to face his demon. To let his own prejudice. <br><br>On the other side, I really love Chloe! This girl is an athlette (soccer too!) and I know that she was though even with all Uilleam's taunting. Chloe is a girl that I want to become BFF with and I think she better with Munro, because Munro respect her, rather than her own mate! Anyhow, I wish that KC don't write her heroines as petite women. I know it's kinda weird. My height just 5 ft, and Chloe is taller than me by 3 inch. But, Uilleam is friggin tall, like almost 7 feet tall, and if I become Chloe, I will feel... dwarfed. Almost all IAD heroines are petite. I don't mind if their height fall into supermodel kind, tho.<br><br>I think that MacRieve like a filler book and the main story is just how Uilleam and Chloe work their messed up relationship. There's no big, bad villain. The villain actually is Uilleam, like what Munro said, for Uilleam's act toward Chloe was kinda unforgivable. That's why he's fallen into unlikable hero in IAD world, lol! The ending kinda have a cliffhanger and heartwrenching too. I want to hug Munro, and I hope he will finally become Lykae that I loved with. There are new Lykaes too, like Ben and Ronan who become comic relief. And some appearance from Chloe's succubus family that finally change Uilleam's view of Chloe.<br><br>Below is my opinion about the cover :P:<br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<b>Update per February, 8th :<br><br>And the cover is finally reveal!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379785628i/472688._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>So :<br><br>- The model head is not cropped. We used to see all his face<br>- He has scruff (yum!) and wear breastplate =&gt; Prefer he shirtless, tho.<br>- His hair is shoulder-length. Why I think he will look like Brad Pitt in Troy? =&gt; Definitely look like Achilles in Troy<br>- I wonder what his eyes colour.. =&gt; Can't decide what colour =&gt; Ahh, we see it now<br>- Judge from his expression, he most likely seems brooding or sulking, lol! =&gt; Most likely tortured. Poor Uilleam<br>- Is it just me or what, but his head look.. smaller than the rest =&gt; I will take it as yes.<br>- Since the model is not Paul Marron, I'll wait the paperback :-)<br><br> </b><br><br><br>Ummm,MacRieve?<br><br>I understand why Lothaire's book called LOTHAIRE, since we all know from the beginning he just known by name "Lothaire" only, not Lothaire Konstantin Daciano. Even this book isabout Uilleam, he's just...not steal attention as big as Lothaire. So, is the naming of this book suit Lothaire's? Sometimes I prefer the previous book title. Maybe this book can be titled like "Dancing with Wolves Prince" or" The Dark Wolf",or something like that.<br>.<br>.<br>.<br>Forget it, anything by Kresley Cole is a must read. And dang, it comes in Hardcover format!! Unless the cover model is Paul Marron again, I will wait the paperback! :(  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><br>Fans of IAD? You will never want to miss this one. And don't call yourself a fans if you not read MacRieve yet!<br><br><b>Favorite scene</b>:<br><br><i>"You've been told that the Pravus males will gang rape you, and still you seek to leave. Mayhap you crave it from them?" He turned and strode away.<br><br>"Prick!" She lined up two balls. Taking aim, she reared back and kicked the first as hard as she could. The second followed in quick succession.<br><br>As planned, the first took him in the back of the head. When he spun around, the second nailed him in the testicles.<br><br>"What...the...fuck?"   <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/466085649?book_show_action=true">Nov 29, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Glamdring" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Glamdring" href="/user/show/6599667-glamdring">Glamdring</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6599667-glamdring?shelf=2013">2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6599667-glamdring?shelf=paranormal-romances">paranormal-romances</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer466085649" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16922486858320544202"><b>*Review without spoiler*</b><br/><br/>MacRieve is the thirteen instalment in the Immortals After Dark series. I’ve been eagerly waiting for this book for 18 months or so. I simply <b>LOVE</b> this series. For me this is one of the best in the paranormal romance genre. I also love Kresley Cole's historical romances, and when I loved her first foray in the YA genre (a genre I really don’t like) I thought that she definitely couldn’t disappoint me whatever she wrote. <br/><br/>I was wrong.<br/><br/>With Shadow’s Claim (The Dacians #1 — a </span>
  <span id="freeText16922486858320544202" style="display:none"><b>*Review without spoiler*</b><br /><br />MacRieve is the thirteen instalment in the Immortals After Dark series. I’ve been eagerly waiting for this book for 18 months or so. I simply <b>LOVE</b> this series. For me this is one of the best in the paranormal romance genre. I also love Kresley Cole's historical romances, and when I loved her first foray in the YA genre (a genre I really don’t like) I thought that she definitely couldn’t disappoint me whatever she wrote. <br /><br />I was wrong.<br /><br />With Shadow’s Claim (The Dacians #1 — a spinoff of the IAD series) and this one, I <i>was</i> disappointed. <br /><br />This book is directly linked to book 11 (Dreams of a Dark Warrior) and it started really good but in the end it didn’t deliver.<br /><br />MacRieve aka Uilleam aka Will aka one half of the Hot and Hotter duet aka head case, is the epitome of the tortured hero. He really had to deal with a lot and I really liked him, even when he wasn’t so nice with Chloe. <br /><br />Chloe starts as a witty, cheeky, strong and resourceful heroine. When something bad happens to her, her motto is “rub some dirt on it and move on”. Unfortunately, as the book went on so did her spunk. <br /><br />The plot didn’t help, simply because there was no plot whatsoever. Worse, there was no action. Furthermore, a lot of things/reactions didn’t make sense for me and there was too many too easy coincidences or about turns. And what happened with Chloe’s father? Really??? <b>*rolls eyes*</b><br /><br />I’m sad to say that the short epilogue with its bloody cliffhanger was more interesting than the book itself. Hopefully, Munro’s book will be better than his twin’s. </span>

          </span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer369854444" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7496975745450005513"><b>5 Hot and Hotter stars</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380742418i/3118026._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>
  <i>"You've let me tend tae your fire, and tonight it's searing me clean. I can be what you need."</i>
</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380742418i/3118027._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>
  <i>He was so domineering. And a dirty talker. Apparently, she liked both. </i>
</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380389135i/750132._SX540_.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380742418ra/3118028.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>That is totally me right now. Yes, fairy wings and all. Why you ask? Well, because I'm fun and eccentric that way. But mainly, it's because I just read a Kresley Cole book and IT.WAS.AWESOME!<br/><br/>I admit that after reading some mixed reviews on this book, I had put off reading it. I have loved every book i th</span>
  <span id="freeText7496975745450005513" style="display:none"><b>5 Hot and Hotter stars</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380742418i/3118026._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <i>"You've let me tend tae your fire, and tonight it's searing me clean. I can be what you need."</i>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380742418i/3118027._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <i>He was so domineering. And a dirty talker. Apparently, she liked both. </i>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380389135i/750132._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380742418ra/3118028.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>That is totally me right now. Yes, fairy wings and all. Why you ask? Well, because I'm fun and eccentric that way. But mainly, it's because I just read a Kresley Cole book and IT.WAS.AWESOME!<br><br>I admit that after reading some mixed reviews on this book, I had put off reading it. I have loved every book i this series, and I was terrified that book 13 might take me off of my IAD buzz.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380742418ra/3118029.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I should have known better. Kresley definitely did not disappoint! MacRieve turned out being so much better than I even hoped. Now this might have been a case of not having any expectations while going into the book. But whatever the reason may have been, I couldn't put it down until I read the very last page.<br><br>The one thing that I have to give praise for, is to this day IAD books continue to focus on only 2 POVs. While there is a whole lot of world building and action that takes place, I never see it take away from the main couple. There are no unnecessary side characters POVs. We get to touch base with many favorite characters, like my personal favorite Nix (and her bat), but the main focus is the couple.<br><br>The one thing that I definitely did notice change, is the books are certainly becoming much more sexual. Or at least this one was. Which you will not find this girl complaining about. But then again, I'm a smut connoisseur :)<br><br>So finally we get the story of the first half of the Hot and Hotter twins, MacRieve. And let me tell you, it was quite brutal. Poor Will has been through quite a bit in his long life, with the recent addition of his stint in The Order's prison and favorite play thing of a demented scientist.<br><br>When he escapes the prison, he's not quite right. And then his life takes a turn when he unexpectedly finds his mate.<br><br>Kresley Cole has yet to write a heroine that I haven't loved, and Chloe was no exception. I loved her sass, and the way she stood up to everyone, even MacRieve.<br><br>Of course we had to get some angst, when a particular secret comes out and throws their mating for a loop. My sexy MacRieve goes from sweet to complete and utter asshole in no time flat.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380742418ra/3118030.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Luckily for me, I like that sort of thing. When the hero makes mistakes and treats the heroine like dirt, but then has to grovel to make up for it? Oh yea! I am ALL over that.<br><br>He also happened to be a dirty talker. Which if you follow my reviews, you know is an Achilles heel of mine. Plus the steam in this book? Sweet mother! I'd say this is the steamiest book in the series. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380742418ra/3118031.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I can see why some reviewers found him to be a little excessive in his anger. but considering his past and what he's been through, I understood it, and it didn't bother me much. Considering that he was able to <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[suppress his beast on a full moon for her <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, which was huge, he did his best to make up for his mistakes with Chloe.<br><br>We also get the set-up for Munro's book, which was a hell of a start. I'm really looking forward to finding out what happens there. But according to Kresley Cole, we will be getting Lanthe and Thronos next. Can't wait to see what that brings. I've been looking forward to their book since Demon From The Dark.<br><br>13 books in the series, and still going strong. This has definitely become one of my favorite PNR series, so a huge rec from me.<br><br>If you like tortured, dirty talking heroes and sassy, strong-willed heroines with fun side characters and amazing world building, snark, humor, and steam, you must check out this series.<br><br>For more reviews visit: <a href="http://dirtygirlromance.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener"> Dirty Girl Romance Book Blog </a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="7496975745450005513" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_619615922" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/619615922" />
    <a title="Melindeeloo" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2766907-melindeeloo"><img alt="Melindeeloo" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1266031818p2/2766907.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/619615922?book_show_action=true">May 19, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Melindeeloo" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Melindeeloo" href="/user/show/2766907-melindeeloo">Melindeeloo</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17378905-macrieve">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2766907-melindeeloo?shelf=shapeshifters">shapeshifters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2766907-melindeeloo?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2766907-melindeeloo?shelf=incubi-and-succubi">incubi-and-succubi</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer619615922&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer619615922" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14489866377406271600">This is completely spoiler ridden - you've been warned.<br/><br/>2 stars = okay. I didn’t hate this book exactly but I didn’t exactly like it either. After a sad little prolog (where a predatory succubus female ensnared the thirteen year old Will resulting in the death of three fifths of his family), and a reminder of what he suffered under the Order’s tender care a couple of books back (vivisection) we get that Will has Issues with a capitol ‘I’. In fact he’s thinking of ending it all until Will goes to </span>
  <span id="freeText14489866377406271600" style="display:none">This is completely spoiler ridden - you've been warned.<br /><br />2 stars = okay. I didn’t hate this book exactly but I didn’t exactly like it either. After a sad little prolog (where a predatory succubus female ensnared the thirteen year old Will resulting in the death of three fifths of his family), and a reminder of what he suffered under the Order’s tender care a couple of books back (vivisection) we get that Will has Issues with a capitol ‘I’. In fact he’s thinking of ending it all until Will goes to an auction where Chloe,the daughter of the hated leader of the Order, is up for sale and Will discovers that Chloe is his mate. Well, it’s an immediate battle for Chloe's life, because all of the Lore wants revenge. In the heat of the conflict, Will's instinct to protect his mate overcomes Cloe’s father's genetic contribution to her existence fairly easily and gives him a new lease on life. <br /><br />After the spending the ‘best day ever’ in his 900 year life with Cloe however, the other half of Chloe’s genes kick in and her mother’s contribution turns Chloe into a succubus and Will into a deplorable bastard, and for an agonizingly long portion of the book Will is absolutely horrible to her. Will can’t quite let Chloe go because his instincts say ‘mine’ and ‘protect’ – but the person she really needs protection from is him and his psychological abuse – and when he finally decides to take a bullet for the team because he can’t let her go and Chloe is starving to death trying to deny her 'hateful nature' and he decides to ‘feed’ her, during their first time together (and her first time ever} Will has to check out and let his ‘beast’ finish the deed and then he vomits immediately afterward – what a nice tender moment. <br /><br />Okay, Chloe is this amazing person and puts enough clues together to figure out the secret Will’s keeping about his childhood and why he hates her race so much, and somehow decides that she loves him – despite his abominable treatment. After impending death for her, he finally has a change of heart when he realizes that he could lose his mate altogether, and he finds out that succubi aren’t all as evil as his first ‘love’, he and Chloe finally have a two sided mating (because succubi have the equivalent of mates too and they don’t drain them dry.) So they live happily ever after, I guess, since instead of a real epilog, we get the teaser for the next book – for MacReive’s brother Munro, who was a super sweetie to Chloe in this book.<br /><br />So, I could have handled the blow up of the conflict between the starring pair a little better if it was a bit more agonizing for Will and a bit less acting out in anger and hatred - Will just lost all of my sympathy at that point. And there really wasn’t enough romance later on in the book to make up for it. Which is too bad, because the relationship is really all that happens in the book and it just isn’t strong enough to be ‘enough’ on its own. This book needed more of something – more Nix or valkyries or more of Chloe's father’s scheme maybe - instead of that we just get Chloe's aunt stepping in with the quick fix info that solves everything.<br /><br />Alrighty then, so all of that makes me sound like I passionately hated this, but actually when I read through it, I was just disconnected. As a result, my resulting ‘meh’ ends up being an ‘okay’ in the star department.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="14489866377406271600" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer14867917518161472537">Reread 5.3.2019 : maybe it's because it's been so long since I read really good pnr but I think I like this way better on second read even though Uillieam- what an asshat! I literally cried in empathy with Chloe. Fact that it moved me is causing me to upgrade my original review from 3 to 4. <br/><br/>Original review:<br/>I liked it okay, still very hot, but I'm getting tired of the "I hate you because you're my enemy, but I want you because you're my mate, but I have to hate you" Cole has going on right now- i</span>
  <span id="freeText14867917518161472537" style="display:none">Reread 5.3.2019 : maybe it's because it's been so long since I read really good pnr but I think I like this way better on second read even though Uillieam- what an asshat! I literally cried in empathy with Chloe. Fact that it moved me is causing me to upgrade my original review from 3 to 4. <br /><br />Original review:<br />I liked it okay, still very hot, but I'm getting tired of the "I hate you because you're my enemy, but I want you because you're my mate, but I have to hate you" Cole has going on right now- in every single release lately. To make things worse, MacRieve has the same theme of one of the pair thinking themselves in love with someone else before they meet their "true mate" and are dogmatic about loving them...even though they're usually secretly evil...and now dead. (Although, granted, MacRieve realizes the former lover is evil before her death but still, the theme <i>is</i> there.)<br /><br /> I liked this series better before she started writing others. It's like she's phoning it in and that just sucks...<br /><br />This one was no different. Ullieam MacRieve has been burned bad in the past when an evil creature he thought was his mate used his beast nature against him. But now he's found his mate, the thing every member of the Lykae dreams of, and she's going to set things right. <br /><br />Of course there's a bump in the road... his mate's new found Lorean (supernatural) nature has come to fore and it's everything that MacRieve hates.<br /><br />As I've stated already parts of this book I thoroughly enjoyed, KC does know how to smex it up, but it in the end I couldnt get passed the been there, read that feel and the fact that the book felt rather short to be a hardback kinda left a bitter taste in my mouth too. <br /><br />I hope she gets back in the game soon... because I love this series too much to give up on it.<br /><br />(Altho from the ending of this one, it looks like Ullieam's twin Munroe's story is shaping up to be exactly the same. <i>sigh</i>)</span>

    <a title="Carmel (Rabid Reads)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4561998-carmel-rabid-reads"><img alt="Carmel (Rabid Reads)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1396922701p2/4561998.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1103487998?book_show_action=true">Nov 11, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Carmel (Rabid Reads)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Carmel (Rabid Reads)" href="/user/show/4561998-carmel-rabid-reads">Carmel (Rabid Reads)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audiobook 9781442353206" href="/book/show/16171826-macrieve">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4561998-carmel-rabid-reads?shelf=audio">audio</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4561998-carmel-rabid-reads?shelf=audio-2015">audio-2015</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1103487998" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4466337707066923409"><b>Reviewed by: <a href='http://rabidreads.ca/2015/12/audiobook-review-macrieve-by-kresley-cole-kresleycole-petkoff-simonaudio.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>Rabid Reads</a>.</b><br/><br/>MACRIEVE had all of the usual components that come standard with every IMMORTALS AFTER DARK installment, but it didn't push the envelope like some of the other volumes have which made it kinda ordinary. I haven't formed much of a connection with the hero over the course of this series, so I didn't have a vested interest in his story going in, and Chloe is a stand-up gal and all, although I did find her too agreeable at times.<br/><br/>In this book Kresley Cole expands upon a supe </span>
  <span id="freeText4466337707066923409" style="display:none"><b>Reviewed by: <a href="http://rabidreads.ca/2015/12/audiobook-review-macrieve-by-kresley-cole-kresleycole-petkoff-simonaudio.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Rabid Reads</a>.</b><br /><br />MACRIEVE had all of the usual components that come standard with every IMMORTALS AFTER DARK installment, but it didn't push the envelope like some of the other volumes have which made it kinda ordinary. I haven't formed much of a connection with the hero over the course of this series, so I didn't have a vested interest in his story going in, and Chloe is a stand-up gal and all, although I did find her too agreeable at times.<br /><br />In this book Kresley Cole expands upon a supe that has yet to take center stage in this series, and normally I'd put a spoiler alert here as it's not mentioned in the blurb; however I'm a late arrival to this world, and therefore the last to know. Anyway, the author did a sweet job of breathing life—or perhaps more aptly put, sex—into her succubi. Her IAD vision never ceases to amaze!<br /><br />I enjoyed learning more the events that have shaped MacRieve, and as usual the interconnectivity between the novels; however I did find that the latter was to a lesser extent than normal which was somewhat disappointing. I also wasn't a huge fan of the ending; Cole hasn't left us in limbo much, so I'm bummed that the next volume isn't about you-know-who after that cliffhanger!<br /><br />Robert Petkoff didn't really have to reinvent the wheel in this installment, but his sexy Scotish werewolf voices will never get old, and he conveyed Chloe's boundless energy very well. There were also a number of never-before-seen secondaries that he had to drum up one-of-a-kind narration for which he of course did with ease, and Nix's cameos continue to be personal favourites.<br /><br />MACRIEVE, despite being about an alpha, was a middle of the pack audiobook.</span>

          </span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16051625-nymeria?shelf=evil-ex">evil-ex</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer664851173" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer2340512825989785325"><a href='http://s808.photobucket.com/user/pommekitty/media/GIFs/tumblr_m8rfpkg9gm1qbffcj_zps5b4d661a.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380428783ra/858249.gif' alt=' photo tumblr_m8rfpkg9gm1qbffcj_zps5b4d661a.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/>Set up: Will MacRieve lived through a traumatic experience with a succubus and was recently tortured at a secret facility run by a certain Commander Webb. <br/><br/>So of course Chloe, his heroine, couldn't be anything other than:<br/><br/>1*a succubus<br/>2*Webb's daughter<br/><br/>My least favorite book in the IAD series.<br/><br/>Will was an asshole for the entire book. Yeah, yeah, poor little Willie has a Sad Past (and said Sad Past was pretty weak compared to what we've previously seen in this series)... Poor little Willie was a p</span>
  <span id="freeText2340512825989785325" style="display:none"><a href="http://s808.photobucket.com/user/pommekitty/media/GIFs/tumblr_m8rfpkg9gm1qbffcj_zps5b4d661a.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380428783ra/858249.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_m8rfpkg9gm1qbffcj_zps5b4d661a.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Set up: Will MacRieve lived through a traumatic experience with a succubus and was recently tortured at a secret facility run by a certain Commander Webb. <br><br>So of course Chloe, his heroine, couldn't be anything other than:<br><br>1*a succubus<br>2*Webb's daughter<br><br>My least favorite book in the IAD series.<br><br>Will was an asshole for the entire book. Yeah, yeah, poor little Willie has a Sad Past (and said Sad Past was pretty weak compared to what we've previously seen in this series)... Poor little Willie was a prejudiced bastard and that's all there was to it. Said prejudiced bastard saw the light (of course) in the blink of an eye at the very end of the book when he's taken to Succubus Land and sees that everybody's nice and harmless. Then he's like: "My wee little mate was innocent all this time? I'm in love!".<br><br>You've got to be kidding me. That's such a huge romance fail. And I'm surprised Cole went this route because she usually has her heroes being slavishly devoted to their heroines, no matter their "evilness" level.<br><br>And I don't know what to think of Chloe. When she learned of his past, she was all "Poor little Willie. No wonder he mistreated / hurt / abused / insulted me all this time. He had just cause. He needs my love. How can I ever make it right for him?" *gah*<br><br>On the other hand, she was kind of stuck in a lose-lose situation: abandoned by her father, having no allies and no clue how to survive in the Lore, getting weaker and weaker etc... Her only way out was Bastard Willie. At least he was supposedly a hot bastard. So, Yay? <br><br>I'm giving this 2 stars because of the entertainment value of reading the scene with Nix driving her Bentley in reverse for miles and miles with her bat Bertil stuck to her chest.<br><br>Here's to hoping Cole will be back on top with the next book in this seemingly neverending series.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer9090541989907675134"><b>Frankly, I'm quite disappointed.</b><br/><br/>I thought that this novel will be as epic as the last one in the series... but sadly, no. :(<br/><br/><br/>Will is a lykae who has a very traumatic past.   <span id="freeText9090541989907675134" style="display:none"><b>Frankly, I'm quite disappointed.</b><br /><br />I thought that this novel will be as epic as the last one in the series... but sadly, no. :(<br /><br /><br />Will is a lykae who has a very traumatic past. PAST being the operative term, lemme just say that he blew this book away in a negative way. Chloe is a professional soccer player who's not really a normal human. A mate that he clearly adored before finding out what she really is. It didn't matter that she really didn't know what she was at first. It didn't matter that he was trash talking an innocent and it didn't matter that he SHAMED HER PUBLICLY. I also do not appreciate and can't get over the "VOMITING" scene. I mean.. <b>VOMITING? REALLY? WTF. WHAT THE HELL IS WRONG WITH YOU??</b> Then when you DECIDE that you believe her, you expect her to fall right head over heels in a click? AFTER ALL THE HUMILIATION? I dunno.. it just.. didn't belong? Hmmm.. <br /><br /><br />This book ended in a good way. However, I feel as if something is missing. My friend who I buddy read with would agree with this: <b>This is not a memorable story.</b><br /><br />I hope that the next one would be better and when I say better, I MEAN REALLY REALLY BETTER.</span>
