    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_440348837" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/440348837" />
    <a title="Taysa" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10540643-taysa"><img alt="Taysa" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353496701p2/10540643.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/440348837?book_show_action=true">Oct 23, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Taysa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Taysa" href="/user/show/10540643-taysa">Taysa</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10540643-taysa?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10540643-taysa?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer440348837" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12196609192314598327">Do you hear that? That is the sound of my heart breaking.<br/><br/>Oh Will! <br/><br/>My initial reaction to reading this book;<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380395271ra/761246.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380395271ra/761247.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>First, let me just say (or rather reiterate) that Kresley is a master story teller. She's got the whole paralell-simultaneous-story-plot-weaving-master-piece thing rocking on. I've read and re-read the IAD series over and again, picking up on new things every time. <br/><br/>But she just completely blew me out of the water (and a little out of my mind) with Will and Chloe's story. <br/><br/>For me, Uilleam and</span>
  <span id="freeText12196609192314598327" style="display:none">Do you hear that? That is the sound of my heart breaking.<br><br>Oh Will! <br><br>My initial reaction to reading this book;<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380395271ra/761246.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380395271ra/761247.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>First, let me just say (or rather reiterate) that Kresley is a master story teller. She's got the whole paralell-simultaneous-story-plot-weaving-master-piece thing rocking on. I've read and re-read the IAD series over and again, picking up on new things every time. <br><br>But she just completely blew me out of the water (and a little out of my mind) with Will and Chloe's story. <br><br>For me, Uilleam and Monroe (the hot and hotter twins) were quietly simmering in the background of the Lore on the cusp of Ascension. I liked them, but I must admit I was hesitant about her announcing that Will would be next in line for a book. <br><br>I was a little more eager for perhaps Lanthe or maybe even Thad. Hell, I wanted Nix!<br><br>But an IAD book was an IAD book, so who was I to scoff at Kresley's brilliant grand plan?<br><br>Never again. I promise, NEVER AGAIN.<br><br>It. Was. BRILLIANT. <br><br>Of course.<br><br>But, it was HEARTBREAKING. Oh, so very heartbreaking.<br><br>Everyone's got issues in life, right? <br><br>WRONG!<br><br>None so much as Will has. Who'd have thought?<br><br>I thought he'd be jovial like Garreth was. <br><br>Nope. <br><br>In the first few pages, I was confused. Then shocked. Then horrified. <br><br>At the end of the first chapter, I was clutching my chest and fighting back sobs; not knowing whether to scream or cry or both.<br><br>Let me just say, it was one of her harder books to read. She writes about a very difficult issue that is both soul shattering and a hard hitting social issue that will mist the eyes of more than one reader. <br><br>If you don't feel for Will while reading this book, I would question your sanity and moral compass.<br><br>Will and Chloe will push some hot topic buttons. In a lot of different ways. <br><br>The story enters into Will's early life and what makes him essentially <i>him</i>. His life is shaped by a not one, but two momentous events that forges a hatred and fire like very few I have read about so far. <br><br>In my personal opinion he comes close to a level of hatred and prejudice akin to Malkom's in <i>Demon from the Dark</i>, but on a very different subject. <br><br>Then on the other hand we have Chloe. Poor, unsuspecting, very human, Chloe. <br><br>She's a bit of a fire cracker and a soccer star with her very own fanboy following. <br><br>We all know Chloe is not what she seems. And eventually she'll have to turn immortal for the progression of this story. I mean, it wouldn't do well to have Will with a human, right? He'd kill her in the first claiming, right?! (Well, this is how I rationalise in my head as I read.)<br><br>Kresley was a tad mysterious in announcing the species of Will's mate. Only saying that her kind hasn't been overly talked about.<br><br>And there is a fair amount of mystery surrounding her identity that will keep you guessing. But due to a little foreshadowing in the first part of the book, most will have the same first guess as me. I'll let you read and find that out for yourself. <br><br>Chloe is pretty cool. She takes a lot of shit in stride with a fantastic attitude. She adopts a soccer (or sports) mentality of when the game (or life) gets rough, you should just rub some dirt in it. Which is a nice way of saying, take a teaspoon of cement and harden the f*ck up. <br><br>Which is great because after her father mysteriously disappears, life turns to shite and she has to more than once adopt the attitude and fight the good fight without breaking down. Hey, if I were in her position, I wouldn't be as brave. <br><br>Then she meets Will and everything is sunshine and daisies for a while.<br><br>And the sunshine and daisy period was lovely. I found myself going back to that part after I had finished. It was like the calm in the storm. A resting stop for the weary traveller. A harbour in a turbulent sea of rocky conflict. Okay, i'll stop the metaphors. <br><br>Actually, it was probably the only time that I really felt at peace with this book. At all other times I was on edge for Will, and on edge for Chloe. <br><br>Because sunshine and daisies turned to dust when Will finally cottons on to her real Lore identity. <br><br>And he goes major psycho. In a really, really bad way. <br><br>But Chloe has no idea <i>what</i> she is, never mind Will's averse reaction to her.<br><br>And it takes a lot of time for Will to come to terms with the demons from his past.<br><br>Kresley writes an emotional roller coaster of breathtaking highs and stomach-pitting lows that left me dizzy and somewhat jarred from her jerky emotional revelations. <br><br>At one moment I was so angry at Will for what he'd said and done to Chloe (mother-trucking bastard!) and then it was all lovey-dovey the next sentence. This is probably the only downside I have to say about this book. Will displays verbally abusive and violent nature that echoes Lachlain's temperament in <i>A Hunger Like No Other</i>. <br><br>And I am not for it, no matter what kind of past you've had Lykae! Chloe is left reeling and confused as to why her once enamoured and charming mate is now ferocious, and not in a good way. But like always, she juts her chin out and hardens up by not taking shit from some over-baring male who won't get with sharing his feelings (you go girl!).<br><br>But not to fret, there is a HEA. Emotions shared, demons conquered, the day is saved!<br><br>It's smart. It's snappy. It's cheesy as all hell, and more than once I was rolling my eyes in amusement for her corny sport references. <br><br>I do think it is a brilliant read that will affect a lot of people in a lot of ways. <br><br>And in an epilogue that will bring back an group of baddies that we have all forgotten about, (and leave you breathless with more questions than answers!) we realise that perhaps Munroe will be next in line for the forthcoming IAD book. Which makes sense, because the twins are so close. <br><br>Overall I am happy, but still somewhat troubled from reading this book. It's a pretty damn powerful story. <br><br>It deserves five stars (because Kresley is awesome), but I fear that it will be received a little less warmly only due to the hard hitting content within. But, the best authors are the ones that make us face issues and think about them long after the last page has turned. <br><br>And you will think on them. <br><br>It is too moving not to.<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="12196609192314598327" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<tr class="no_border feedFooterReview" id="update_comment_stuff_Review440348837">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Anna (Bobs Her Hair)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Anna (Bobs Her Hair)" href="/user/show/3167458-anna-bobs-her-hair">Anna (Bobs Her Hair)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17378905-macrieve">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Paranormal Romance Fans</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3167458-anna-bobs-her-hair?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer386494782" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9802418873605536679"><b>4.5 stars or A</b><br/><br/>This books packs an emotional wallop. Will the lycae mates ever catch a break? They werewolves are always paired with someone who pushes them to their limit. <br/><br/>Chloe is a human, or so she believes. Her father's secrets come out and there's more to learn. The most devastating story belongs to MacRieve. It's tragic and I wonder why I never really noticed his character with the exception of the 'hot and hotter' nickname. <br/><br/>This book has a different feel compared to the other IAD books. It</span>
  <span id="freeText9802418873605536679" style="display:none"><b>4.5 stars or A</b><br /><br />This books packs an emotional wallop. Will the lycae mates ever catch a break? They werewolves are always paired with someone who pushes them to their limit. <br /><br />Chloe is a human, or so she believes. Her father's secrets come out and there's more to learn. The most devastating story belongs to MacRieve. It's tragic and I wonder why I never really noticed his character with the exception of the 'hot and hotter' nickname. <br /><br />This book has a different feel compared to the other IAD books. It's quieter. Not the action packed adventure in No Rest for the Wicked. Where the action is missing there is subtler story told. For me, this book is another winner by Kresley Cole. Those that felt pushed away by Lothaire's over-the-top antics may find emotional thread in MacRieve more to their liking. <br /><br /></span>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText17988727829970444241" style="display:none"><b>3.5 Stars</b><br /><br />I mostly enjoyed this but it definitely won't go down in my list of favorites. <br /><br />I was really liking the first half of the story...there was some good sexual tension and I was enjoying watching MacRieve try to woo Chloe. MacRieve had one of the saddest prologues I've ever read. And then add the things that Webb and Dixon did him...I just wanted him to have a great story. Sadly, it all kinda went to hell in the second half, pretty much exactly how I predicted. It was very frustrating for me to read about MacRieve hating Chloe and some of the things he said to her...then over night he does a 180 and wants to make it work! WTF?!   <span id="freeText6232140734784392" style="display:none">Fantasy romance series. <br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ For mature audiences. <br>The beginning of this story was appalling. Love saves Uilleam. <br>Each novel in this series is about different partners, with different powers. The panoramic view of the story is that a big war between immortals called The Ascension will eventually take place and many immortals will die. Good and bad. <div id="review_1943097435" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1943097435" />
    <a title="AJ" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3143126-aj"><img alt="AJ" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1406382884p2/3143126.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1943097435?book_show_action=true">Mar 20, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="AJ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="AJ" href="/user/show/3143126-aj">AJ</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=lol">lol</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=romantic">romantic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=audio">audio</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=feeeeels">feeeeels</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=paranormal-uf">paranormal-uf</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1943097435" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4649499186670468931"><b><i>“Where your mate goes, you follow. . . .” </i><br/><br/>4.5 stars!</b><br/> <br/>I love this series, and I love this paranormal world! With a wonderful collection of supernatural creatures, Kresley Cole has created a fantastically complex world that I love to lose myself in, and each story is exciting and intriguing, laugh-out-loud funny, sexy and romantic with great action. I absolutely love these books, and I loved finally getting the story of broody lykae badass, Uilleam MacRieve.<br/> <br/>Uilleam is a lykae chief, and cousin to</span>
  <span id="freeText4649499186670468931" style="display:none"><b><i>“Where your mate goes, you follow. . . .” </i><br><br>4.5 stars!</b><br> <br>I love this series, and I love this paranormal world! With a wonderful collection of supernatural creatures, Kresley Cole has created a fantastically complex world that I love to lose myself in, and each story is exciting and intriguing, laugh-out-loud funny, sexy and romantic with great action. I absolutely love these books, and I loved finally getting the story of broody lykae badass, Uilleam MacRieve.<br> <br>Uilleam is a lykae chief, and cousin to the MacRieves we have already met in the series (Lachlain, Garreth and Bowen). He’s been through hell, is fairly antisocial and a bit of a loner and a manwhore and, together with his twin brother, Munro, they are known as ‘Hot’ and ‘Hotter’ (though they argue which of them owns which title). <br> <br>Chloe is a professional soccer player known as ‘Baby T-Rex’. She’s smart, fierce, sassy and no-nonsense, and is absolutely driven to achieve her dreams of sporting glory. But her whole life is ripped out from under her when she is taken from her home and ends up on the supernatural auction block. Surrounded by creatures from myth and legend, she has no idea what is happening to her and what she’s in for, and then she is rescued by a big, burly Scot who claims her as his own.<br> <br>MacRieve recognises Chloe as his fated mate before he even lays eyes on her. Unlike his brother, he has never longed for his mate, he doesn’t want one, and he doesn’t feel worthy of having one – his past leaving him terrified of falling so completely, or of having a lasting bond with somebody. The fact that she is human is also a problem. But from the moment he is with her, he is enamoured. She is his life, his reason for living, and he will do anything to protect her and make her happy, and OMG, it’s beautiful to see!!!!<br> <br><blockquote>
  <i>“You asked me how old I am I was born roughly nine centuries ago. I’ve lived for more than three hundred thousand days. And you made this one my favorite one of all.” </i>
</blockquote><br>*dreamy sigh*<br> <br>Chloe adjusts surprisingly well to MacRieve. Of course she’s terrified, but he is a gentle giant, soothing her and opening his heart to her, and she finds him impossible to resist. It helps that he’s sexy as all hell, of course, and the steamy time is both sizzling and beautifully emotional.<br> <br><blockquote>
  <i>“She pressed a single soft kiss over his heart, having no idea he’d just given it to her.”</i>
</blockquote><br>But their coming together unleashes something unexpected. Something that changes everything, setting their lives on a completely different path as MacRieve is forced to relive is personal hell and Chloe is left to come to terms with not only who she is, but the fact that her brand new mate that she was so quickly falling for, is now a very real danger to her. <br> <br>OMG, this book took my emotions for a ride! I guessed where it was going to go, but I wasn’t expecting the intensity of the fallout, and OMG, the feels!!!<br> <br>For a start, MacRieve’s backstory broke my heart. His childhood was tragic, and then he was one of those who were captured by The Order and subjected to all kinds of brutal torture which re-opened his emotional and psychological wounds and left him a shattered shell of who he once was. And then Chloe came into his life and I was flying high watching them fall for each other so beautifully. But then it all turns to hell, and I was so, so pissed as it all went down. I could rant on and on about the unfairness, cruelty, viciousness, betrayal and appalling behaviour that went on (it’s been a few days, and I’m clearly still all riled up about it). It’s not the story I wanted for them, and my heart broke at how it all played out, but I was glued to every moment. It sets up a wonderfully complex dynamic as their intense connection to each other is pitted against all of the drama between them, and it creates a huge emotional hurdle for them to overcome and fight back from, and <i>that</i> was fantastic to see. <br> <br><blockquote>
  <i>“I know I’m wrong in the head! I want to be . . . right. For you.” </i>
</blockquote><br> Let’s take a moment to celebrate the awesomeness of Chloe, because even with all that she goes through, her strength and sass is absolutely sensational! She stands up to MacRieve when she should have been terrified, and I cheered over and over for her! She is smart-mouthed with a wicked sense of humour, and she’s completely emotionally open, accepting and forgiving and I love that she never held anything back. Her determination to push through all that she was going through when she would have been well within her rights to curl up into a ball in the corner and just weep is fantastic, and on top of it all she’s funny as all hell. I absolutely love her, and I have the biggest girl-crush on her.<br> <br><blockquote> <i>“Now, why don’t you shove in a manpon and tug up your manties” </i>
</blockquote><br> She’s a wonderful match for MacRieve, and even though it hurt, I loved their story.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“Where your mate goes, you follow. . . .” </i>
</blockquote><br>As always, one of the highlights of this book for me was the extended cast of characters. Nix is crazy perfection and always makes me laugh, but it was the band of lykae that I really loved. Munro is a fantastic character, and I love his strength and his sweet nature, and the two teenagers that the brothers have taken into their home were an absolute riot! I loved their antics and their hilarious banter, which provided a great sense of balance to the intensity of the rest of the story. <br> <br>The story ends in a great place, but on a bit of a cliffhanger for another book to come with the epilogue giving us a glimpse into Munro’s story, and it looks like it’s going to be a great one! I can’t wait to get to it. <br> <br>I loved this book. Drama, humour, sexy romance and twists and turns galore – it hurt, but it was so, so good! 4.5 stars. <br> <br>And bravo once again to Robert Petkoff who is absolutely perfection in narrating this audiobook.<br><br><br><a href="http://www.escapistbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1459520401i/18621730.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="4649499186670468931" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1612377803" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1612377803" />
    <a title="Candace" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16384209-candace"><img alt="Candace" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1459720769p2/16384209.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1612377803?book_show_action=true">Apr 16, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Candace" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Candace" href="/user/show/16384209-candace">Candace</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17378905-macrieve">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=listened-to-audio-version">listened-to-audio-version</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=age-difference">age-difference</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=dangerous-hero-themed-books-read">dangerous-hero-themed-books-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=kidnapped">kidnapped</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1612377803" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5976803894715799538">Listening to the books in this series back to back, without the wait for each new release, has been both absorbing and tedious at times. On the one hand, I am completely enthralled with this series and having to wait for the next book might kill me. On the other hand, there are so many similarities between the books that they can begin to feel unoriginal and redundant.<br/><br/>That being said, this was not one of my favorites in the series. I liked the story of Uilleam, aka "Will", MacRieve and Chloe, bu</span>
  <span id="freeText5976803894715799538" style="display:none">Listening to the books in this series back to back, without the wait for each new release, has been both absorbing and tedious at times. On the one hand, I am completely enthralled with this series and having to wait for the next book might kill me. On the other hand, there are so many similarities between the books that they can begin to feel unoriginal and redundant.<br /><br />That being said, this was not one of my favorites in the series. I liked the story of Uilleam, aka "Will", MacRieve and Chloe, but I didn't love it. I give it 3 1/2 stars rounded up, but I could have just as easily rounded this one down.<br /><br />When Will first recognizes Chloe Todd as his mate, she's about to be auctioned off as a tool for revenge against her father. The daughter of Webb, one of The Order's highest ranking officials, Chloe has unwittingly become a pawn in the war between The Order and the supernatural beings of the lore. There is no shortage of beings that would like to torture Chloe in the same manner in which her father so cruelly tortured them. Will rescues Chloe from the unspeakable, risking his own life to snatch her from the grasp of the winning bidder.<br /><br />During the days immediately following her rescue, Will is the perfect gentleman. He treats Chloe like a queen, doing his best to woo her and win her affections. I thought that Will was going to be a new favorite of mine at this point.<br /><br />Then, when it turned out that "human" Chloe wasn't quite so human after all, Will turned into a complete ass. This is where things started to fall apart for me. As Chloe began her transition as a succubus, Will treated her as if she were an abomination. From one extreme to the next, he left my head spinning.<br /><br />While I understood that he had suffered greatly at the hands of another succubus in his youth, that certainly had nothing to do with poor Chloe. Yet, he repeatedly made her pay for the wrongs of another. He turned from Prince Charming into an abusive, cruel bastard in the blink of an eye. <br /><br />From that point forward, I couldn't really forgive Will. I pretty much wrote him off and there was oncoming back for him. As far as he was concerned, I was done. Put a fork in it!<br /><br />Despite Will's lack of appeal, I did love Chloe and Will's brother, Munro. Too bad those two couldn't have been matched up. I would have been much happier if they had!<br /><br />Chloe was a strong, sassy heroine. Even though she was stuck with Will the super-jerk, she didn't wallow around in misery or allow him to abuse her. She stood up for herself and gave as good as she got. <br /><br />Throughout it all, Munro was the voice of reason. He provided Chloe with support and a safe haven when her own mate sought to harm her. He tried to make Will see the error of his ways, though his efforts were futile. He even intervened to protect Chloe from his brother. Munro was the real hero in this story if you ask me!<br /><br />Overall, I enjoyed the story, but not in the way I'd expected. This time around, I found myself frustrated with the love story. It was the backstory and the supporting characters and relationships that salvaged this one for me. In the end, it was alright.<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="5976803894715799538" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('jZ7ALlj7X7YEOrBsk9gVxpEWTVjsEkIsuiSbMaC72hFFCIjr0kdJoJQDHAt51xUgShnAClYCkWp8QhRg9Z4CLw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  }

  <span id="freeText18403903080016522341" style="display:none">Kresley Cole is the #1 <i>New York Times</i> bestselling author of the electrifying Immortals After Dark paranormal series, the young adult Arcana Chronicles series, the erotic Gamemakers series, and five award-winning historical romances.<br /><br />A master’s grad and former athlete, she has traveled over much of the world and draws from those experiences to create her memorable characters and settings. <br />Her IAD books have been translated into 23 foreign languages, garnered three RITA awards, a RWA Hall of Fame induction, and consistently appear on the bestseller lists, in the U.S. and abroad.<br /><br />Cole lives in Florida with her family. Learn more about Kresley at: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.kresleycole.com">www.kresleycole.com</a> &amp; <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.thearcanachronicles.com">www.thearcanachronicles.com</a><br /><br /></span>
